if more than 1 team tied with same number of points, these rules shall be followed: 1. Past head to head result in the tournament in both rounds would apply. A team with win over the other tied team in the point table will go above the other team which lost in prior match(es). 2. If equal, higher number of wins  3. If still equal, net run rate  4. If still equal, lower bowling strike rate So CK in BB out :) Bad luck for BB & Good luck for CK.
